Retrial of Former Mixed Court Cases by the First Special Court 142

Some to Be Released Immediately

Some to Have Original Sentences Upheld

Murderer Subject to Increased Sentence

The Shanghai First Special District Court, due to the illegality of the former Mixed Court's jury verdicts in English, has recently decided to rehear all uncompleted cases of this type to rectify them. Yesterday morning, Judge Feng Shide of the court issued new verdicts in four more cases. Deng Haizhou and three others were sentenced to ten years in the Western prison on December 18th of the 13th year of the Republic for robbery. Among them, Liu, Wang, and Dong were released early based on the old regulations due to their remorse in prison and adherence to prison rules, according to the Western prison officials. Only Deng Haizhou remained, and according to the original sentence calculation, he was scheduled to be released on July 1st. Now, Judge Feng has changed the sentence to five years of imprisonment. Because the police lawyer Wang Yaotang declared the abandonment of the appeal, he was released in court immediately. (2) Lin Laowu and Chen Yunxiang were also sentenced to fifteen years each on October 15th of the 14th year of the Republic for robbery. Now, the sentence has been changed to eight years each, but the police lawyer has reserved the right to appeal, so this verdict is not yet considered final. (3) Guan Chaoyuan was sentenced to ten years for murder, and he is still sentenced to ten years, but the crime seems to be slightly different from before. (4) Yu Laifa was also convicted of murder and sentenced to ten years. Judge Feng reviewed the case and considered the previous sentence too light to atone for the crime, so he changed the sentence to fifteen years and advised that an appeal could be made according to the law. It has been found that more than ten cases have been reheard, and Yu Laifa is the first to have his sentence increased.

A Tale of Woe (啼笑因緣) Dispute 143

The Mingxing Film Company's production of the play "A Tale of Woe" has been in litigation with the Dahua Film Company for a long time over the issue of the screenplay registration and filming rights, but no satisfactory solution has been reached. Both sides are actively engaged in filming, sparing no effort. Recently, Mingxing Film Company has completed the first part of the play and screened it at the Nanjing Grand Theatre on Edward Road a few days ago. For days, crowds flocked to see it, and every performance was packed. Dahua Company Manager Gu Wuwei believes that the film adaptation rights of "A Tale of Woe" have been registered and approved by the Ministry of Interior, and the business is at stake, so he cannot allow other companies to remake and screen it. He filed a petition with the Second Special District Court the day before yesterday, willing to provide a guarantee to prohibit the screening of the film before a verdict is issued. After the petition was submitted the day before yesterday, the court did not issue the preliminary attachment order because of the late hour. It was not until 11:00 a.m. yesterday that the court issued it. Judicial police arrived at the Nanjing Grand Theatre at about 12:00 noon with the order, ordering it to stop the screening immediately. Mingxing Company Manager Zhang Shichuan went to the Second District Court to state the reasons and expressed willingness to provide a guarantee. The Second District Civil Court immediately approved the continuation of the screening, so the Nanjing Grand Theatre still screened "A Tale of Woe" three times yesterday at 3:00 p.m., 5:30 p.m., and 9:15 p.m. without stopping. However, starting today, the Mingxing side will automatically stop the screening and await a legal resolution.

The New Pharmaceutical Association First Purchases

Formal Establishment of Chinese Military Music 145

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce established Chinese military music, which was formally established the day before yesterday. There are a total of 60 members in the team and 20 reserves. Every Tuesday and Thursday evening from 7:00 p.m. to 9:00 p.m., they will be formally trained in the conference hall of the Chamber of Commerce. Zheng Jinwen is the general instructor, and Xu Ruhui and others are assistant teachers. The musical instruments are divided into four categories: (wind), (string), (bowed), and (percussion), with a total of 32 kinds. All team members are able to study seriously, and future achievements can be guaranteed. The first step in training is to start with the flute as a basic exercise. Once there is some progress, they will be divided into classes for specialized study. All musical instruments are manufactured by the Datong Music Society, with the standard of being light and easy to carry. The music used is based on folk songs. That night, each person was given a xiao and a flute, and the timbre was uniform. In addition, the musical instruments are being rushed to be made, and they will be completed by mid-next month. In the future, the provinces will follow suit, and the scale will be even greater.

Record of the Welcome Meeting at the Guangzhao Public Association 146

All Had Earnest Speeches Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 p.m., the Shanghai Guangzhao Public Association specially held a tea party to welcome philanthropists Chen Lianbo, Zhou Shouchen, Cai Chang, and Li Yutang. Guests included Zhu Qinglan, Zhang Peiyan, Cha Liangzhao, Yan Zhifang, Chen Jintao, Wen Yingxing, Cai Zengji, and directors and councilors of the association. It was quite a grand occasion. At 5:00 p.m., the guests and hosts dispersed in joy. The speeches of Wen, Chen, and Cai are listed below:

Wen Zongyao's Speech: Mr. Chen Lianbo, Chairman of the Tung Wah Hospital in Hong Kong, Sir Zhou Shouchen, Chinese Representative of the Legislative Council, and Mr. Cai Chang, Chairman of the Guangzhou Convenience Hospital, have come to Shanghai for official business, allowing us to take this opportunity to hold a meeting here to welcome and thank them in person. It is extremely gratifying. Everyone in Guangdong knows that you are tireless in doing good deeds and courageous in doing what is right. During the Shanghai war, you raised huge sums of money in Hong Kong and Guangzhou and remitted them to Shanghai, which was not only enough to relieve the refugees, but also had a surplus to help various hospitals and schools. All the compatriots in Shanghai are deeply grateful. On behalf of all the beneficiaries, I thank you. Although the Shanghai war lasted only a little over a month and the area was only Songhu, the planes and fierce cannons were even worse than the invasion of Beijing by the Eight-Nation Alliance in the Gengzi year. It is estimated that more than 240,000 compatriots died, and Guangdong people accounted for one-third of them. The Shanghai Municipal Council (SMC) cannot escape its responsibility for this matter. After the incident, I personally inquired about everything. According to the investigation, Japan had already decided to open fire that night, regardless of whether we accepted its conditions or not. The SMC knew this a long time ago, but because none of the five Chinese directors of the SMC were from Guangdong, the news was blocked and they did not know the situation, which was one of the reasons for the disaster. There are more than 200,000 Guangdong people in Shanghai, and everything the SMC does has a close relationship with them, but there is no representative from Guangdong among the Chinese directors, which is the most strange and unfair thing. Our compatriots in Shanghai should stand up and fight for it. Starting from the next session, at least one of the five Chinese directors of the SMC must be a representative from Guangdong. This is the minimum limit. This intention should be stated to the Chinese Ratepayers' Association. In the early days of the establishment of the Chinese directors of the SMC, Huang Mingdao, the manager of the Xinhua Bank, was elected as a Chinese director to represent the Guangdong people. Later, Mr. Huang resigned due to disagreement, and there has been no representative from Guangdong since then. Now Guo Shun has been elected as an advisor, but the status of a Chinese advisor is very different from that of a Chinese director. Our Guangdong people must pay attention. This time, our compatriots have been spared from being displaced thanks to your help, and we are as grateful as if we have been reborn. At this point, the chairman asked everyone to stand up and express their gratitude to Mr. Chen and others, and wish them good health.

Chen Lianbo's Speech: After the Shanghai incident, all Guangdong people were worried because most of our Guangdong compatriots in Shanghai lived in the Zhabei area, so they were all in a state of anxiety. At that time, there was already an organization of the Guangdong Compatriots Relief Association in Shanghai. We then initiated a fundraising with various gentry and merchants. However, we were just spending more effort for our fellow villagers. We are comfortable in Hong Kong and Guangdong and feel guilty for not being able to do more. How dare we speak of merit? Looking at this war of resistance against Japan, the Guangdong people are the ones who are leading the charge, and the Guangdong people are the ones who are relieving the refugees. In all righteous deeds, the Guangdong people can die for the country. In this time of national crisis, it is especially important to unite and combine the compatriots in Shanghai, Hong Kong, and Guangdong into one, so that the success in the future will be limitless.

Cai Chang's Speech: Whenever there are disasters in Guangdong Province, the funds raised locally are insufficient, and we rely on the donations of compatriots in Shanghai, Hankou, and overseas. I am very sorry. During this Shanghai incident, Guangzhou raised little money due to the depression in the market, but it was only a small effort. However, Hong Kong is relatively affluent, so it was able to raise huge sums of money. The Convenience Hospital has no savings and relies only on donations, but the money donated is enough to cover the expenses. Therefore, this time it has accommodated more than 15,000 refugees sent back to Guangdong from Shanghai. In addition to sending them back to their hometowns, each person was given four yuan. This amount of money is also very large. At present, there are 300 to 400 refugees who have returned to Guangdong and plan to return to Shanghai to work. They are all funded by the Convenience Hospital to go to Shanghai, and each person is given ten yuan so that they will not be in poverty after arriving in Shanghai. In the future, I hope that all compatriots in the province and abroad will unite in the face of disasters and devote themselves to relief work. I especially hope that the compatriots in Shanghai will work together in harmony to receive the help of Heaven and help themselves.

Opening of the Zhonghe Bulb Company Today 148

General Electric, Osram, and Philips are the Best-Selling Bulbs in the World. In order to reduce manufacturing costs and save on distribution expenses, a joint organization distribution office has been established in China, named Zhonghe Bulb Company. The address is temporarily set at 49 Beijing Road, and business will begin on July 1st. Tea and refreshments are specially prepared to invite Shanghai's electrical industry colleagues and all walks of life. The past history and recent business overview of the three companies are briefly described below: (1) General Electric Edison. The American General Electric Company has been in business for more than 50 years since Edison invented the bulb. It has been improved and refined, and its branches are all over the world. The General Electric Edison Factory in Shanghai was founded 15 years ago by the current general manager Pan Qijun. It covers an area of 130 mu and has more than 1,000 workers. In addition to manufacturing electrical materials, it can now produce 40,000 light bulbs per day. (2) Osram. The Berlin Osram Factory in Germany was formed in 1919 by the merger of three bulb factories: Siemens, AEG, and others. At that time, the three factories had 30 years of experience in manufacturing bulbs. Osram is the largest bulb factory in the world outside of the United States. It sells well all over the world. In addition to the three main factories in Berlin, there are 10 branches in various parts of Europe. In addition, there are affiliated glass factories, coal factories, and machine factories, which are not included. The Berlin headquarters is now equipped with several new machines for manufacturing glass bulbs, each of which can produce 50,000 bulbs per day. In 1930, the total output of Osram was 120 million bulbs, which were distributed all over the world. Users all praised it. (3) Philips. The Philips Bulb Factory is the largest factory in the Netherlands. It was founded in 1891 by electrical engineer Mr. Philips. It has been expanded and now has 20,000 workers. It can produce 70 million bulbs per year. The factory is located in the southern part of the Netherlands. All glass, filaments, cardboard boxes, and other parts for manufacturing bulbs are manufactured by Philips in its own factory. It also has a very large research institute, which is the leading one in Europe and is famous all over the world. (4) The contents of the Zhonghe Bulb Company. The Zhonghe Bulb Company has now hired Mr. Macy, formerly of the Philips Foreign Firm, as the general manager. Mr. Macy founded the Shanghai Philips Foreign Firm and has been engaged in the bulb business for ten years. In addition, Mr. Cliff, formerly of the General Electric Edison Company, has been hired as the manager of the sales department, and Mr. Russell, formerly of the Osram Foreign Firm, has been hired as the manager of the general affairs department. The three gentlemen are all experienced. They have now joined the new company, and Pan Qijun, the general manager of the Edison Factory, can also assist from time to time. In the future, the business will definitely flourish and will be of considerable assistance to the progress of China's electrical industry.

Large-Scale Opium Organization Verdict on North Sichuan Road 149

The police officers Zhao Bingkun and Song Bingzheng and the Western detective Pan Gensi of the Narcotics Department of the Public Concession Police, previously cracked a large-scale chain of opium selling organizations at 690, 706, and 714 Renzhi Lane on North Sichuan Road. They arrested four people, including Cantonese woman Tan Yuelan, Wang Zhen, and related persons Li Pei and Liang Song, and seized a large amount of opium and opium paste, totaling more than 400 taels, as well as smoking utensils, account books, and notebooks. They were taken to the Hongkou Police Station for investigation. It was found that the main culprit, Liu Wenzhong, had fled back to his hometown. The four men and women were sent to the First Special District Court for interrogation and concluded. Yesterday morning, Judge Shen Bingrong pronounced the verdict in Court No. 1. Tan Yuelan was sentenced to six months of imprisonment and a fine of 2,000 yuan for helping to sell opium. She was fined 300 yuan for possessing utensils exclusively for eating opium. The sentence to be executed is six months of imprisonment and an amount of 2,200 yuan. Wang Zhen was sentenced to six months of imprisonment and a fine of 2,000 yuan for helping to sell opium. If the fine is not paid after compulsory execution, the total amount of the fine shall be converted proportionally to the number of days in a year. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined shall be offset against one day of imprisonment every two days. Li Pei and Liang Song were fined 300 yuan each for possessing opium. If they are converted to detention, they shall be converted at the rate of two yuan per day. The opium and opium paste shall be confiscated according to the list.

Railway Bi-Weekly with a Renewed Look 150

The first issue of the second volume is published. The Railway Bi-Weekly, edited and published by the Chinese Railway Transportation Society and edited by railway expert Zheng Baozhao, has published 14 issues since its founding. From the 15th to the 36th issue, it is a special issue on the problem of railway organization in China, which brings together the writings of famous experts, totaling 300,000 words. It has been sent to the printing press and is about to be completed. Suddenly, the Shanghai Incident occurred, and the printing was in the war zone, so the original manuscripts were all burned. In addition to the Society separately collecting and planning to reprint, the first issue of the second volume of this year is scheduled to be published on July 1. The content and appearance have been greatly updated. Important texts include "The Knowledge that Railway Youths Should Have," "The Prerequisites for Implementing Responsible Transportation in State-Owned Railways," "A Plan for Establishing a Business Office for State-Owned Railway Vehicle Operations," "An Overview of the American Railway Sleeping Car Bed Reservation System," and "An Overview of the Two Railways Before and After the January 28th Incident." There are also other road event summaries, book reviews, etc., which are mostly carefully written and invaluable works. The trial reading is attached with a one-cent postage stamp. The distribution department is located at 686 Kangle Lane, Kangnaogang Road, Shanghai. The magazine welcomes contributions from all walks of life. All manuscripts on railway management, engineering, machinery, and materials are being collected. After publication, the remuneration will be generous. The pieces should be sent to the Editorial Department of the magazine at 198 Hekang Lane, Dagu Road, Shanghai.

Inspection Report of the Bank of China 151

The 52nd Inspection Report of the Shanghai Bank of China Issuance Reserve Inspection Committee states that the committee members and entrusted accountants, in accordance with the rules of the committee, inspected the Shanghai Bank of China's own issuance and interbank exchange coupon reserve treasury on June 26, 1932, and held the 52nd inspection at the bank. The Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance also joined the inspection. The results of the inspection are listed below: The total amount of exchange coupons issued is 99,453,566 yuan, including 52,983,362 yuan issued by the bank, 18,498,380 yuan used by interbanks, and 27,971,824 yuan used by various banks and shops. Except for the portion used by various banks and shops, which will be inspected separately according to the original method, the inspection of the interbank portion is as follows: The amount of exchange coupons issued by the bank and used by interbanks is 71,481,742 yuan. The amount of reserve for the bank's and interbanks' exchange coupons is 71,481,742 yuan, including 43,191,659.24 yuan in cash reserve and 28,290,082.76 yuan in guarantee reserve. The above two items, the cash reserve accounts for 60% and the guarantee reserve accounts for 40%, and the inspection is accurate as stated. In accordance with Article 5 of the rules, this is a formal report. June 26, 1932, Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance, Xu Kan, Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce Representatives Pei Yunqing, Wang Yansong, Shanghai Banking Association Representatives Ye Fuxiao, Tang Shoumin, Shanghai Money Industry Association Representatives Fu Songnian, Li Jisheng, Representatives of Banks and Shops Holding Coupons Le Gengrong, Xi Qisun, Representatives of Directors and Supervisors of the Bank of China Ye Zhuotang, Zhou Zongliang, Xu Jiliang, Li Zhilian, Accountant Wang Zikang.

Dog Owners Must Obtain Licenses 155

All dog owners who have not yet obtained a license this year must immediately go to the Municipal Council's Donation Office to apply for one. The license fee is five yuan per dog. Dog owners who take their dogs to the road or other public places must have them wear a proper muzzle, but it must not interfere with the dog's breathing and drinking water. If dogs without muzzles are found in public places, whether or not they are being carried by someone, they will be captured by patrols and sent to the dog pound for detention for at least one week. If their owners are found, they will be prosecuted. Dogs whose muzzles are not effective will be treated as if they have no muzzles. Dogs without muzzles may be shot if they cannot be captured. Dog owners are requested to pay close attention to this matter.

False Counterfeiting of Earp Electrical Products Discovered 160

The electric fans, light bulbs, motors, electric stoves, and other products manufactured by the Earp Electrical Factory are of excellent quality and sell well both domestically and abroad, having been in business for many years. Recently, some unscrupulous merchants, seeing this success, have coveted it and have been passing off inferior goods as Earp-branded light bulbs, selling them in various locations. After reports were received from the factory's various regional management offices via letters and telegrams, the factory specifically offered a reward of one thousand yuan in the "Shen Bao," "Xin Bao," and other newspapers to investigate and apprehend the culprits in order to maintain the reputation of its products and avoid any impact on its business.

Important Education News

Hunan Province Holds Graduation Examinations 162

Students Request the Withdrawal of the Order. A Changsha dispatch states that the Hunan Education Department, acting on the order of the Ministry of Education to hold graduation examinations for students, proposed at the first meeting to establish the "Hunan Middle School Graduation Examination Committee" and hired fourteen people, including Huang Shiheng and Ou Minggao, as committee members. The designated subjects for the examinations are as follows: For senior high school, Party Principles, Chinese Language, Mathematics, History, Geography, Chemistry, Biology, Foreign Language, Physical Education, and ten other subjects. For junior high school, Party Principles, Chinese Language, Mathematics, History, Geography, Nature, Physical Education, Foreign Language, and eight other subjects. For all students taking the examination, it is stipulated that if a student fails in one or two subjects, they may retake the failed subjects once. If the retake is still unsuccessful, they are allowed to take a remedial course for one academic year and participate in the examination for those subjects again during the next term, but only once. Those who fail in three or more subjects will be required to repeat the grade. Due to the approaching summer vacation and the pressing time constraints, preparations are being actively carried out, and a founding meeting will be held at the Education Department at 2:00 PM today to complete the arrangements within two weeks. Upon hearing the news, the graduating students from over ten schools, including Hunan University, No. 1 Middle School, No. 1 Normal School, Mingde, Qunfa, Agricultural Vocational School, and Duize, totaling approximately 1,500 people, each appointed representatives to hold a joint meeting at the Education Association and decided to express the difficulties of the examination and request the provincial government to withdraw the order. The reasons they hold are as follows: (1) Each school follows the Ministry's order of the 18th year of the Republic and divides into Arts and Science disciplines. This examination did not differentiate them, and the nature of the subjects before and after is naturally different. (2) The examination order was only announced in the past two days. To test three years' worth of subjects in one day is neither permitted by time nor by mental capacity. (3) Entrance examinations for various universities in the country, such as Nanjing University, will be held as early as July 3rd. Other universities, such as Wuhan University, mostly start registration in early July, with no extensions. It seems inappropriate to hinder the opportunity for higher education with the examination. (4) The examination has not been held in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, which proves that it is difficult to comply with this order before the middle school curriculum system is unified. Not only do middle schools in our province have different curriculums, but their teaching is also independently administered. Since they all share this special situation, they should be treated the same way. (5) The Ministry of Education also considered the difficulties of suddenly holding this examination this term and clearly ordered each province that, if there are special circumstances that prevent the examination from being held, they can report it for record-keeping and be exempted from holding it, leaving room for flexibility. Since our province has such difficulties, it should be included in the list of exemptions from the examination. (6) Senior high schools in this province generally implement a credit system. Once the credits are completed, students can graduate. Now that the required credits have been completed, it seems unnecessary to participate in this examination according to the regulations. At the same time, they also sent a letter to the Student Union, asking it to forward the request to the Provincial Party Department to send a letter requesting exemption from the examination. However, the Provincial Government believes that this examination is imperative and will not be cancelled due to students' requests.

Ministry of Education Revises Short-Term Elementary School Curriculum Standards 163

The short-term elementary school curriculum standards promulgated by the Ministry of Education were seen in yesterday's newspaper. Now, the Ministry of Education has slightly revised them. The content of the curriculum remains the same as the original, but in the first paragraph of the second article on objectives, "leadership" is changed to "promotion," and the second paragraph is changed to "imparting basic knowledge of local autonomy and practicing four types of application in order to expand the civil rights movement." In the curriculum content, under A. regarding moral education, "center" is changed to "subject," and (4) is changed to "in the arithmetic class, practicing precise and correct thinking to promote the practice of morality." B. "demonstration" is changed to "example." The rest remains the same as the original.

Ministry of Education Cables to Stop Foreigners Without Passports from Entering the Country 164

The Ministry of Education, based on a telegram from five cultural institutions in Beiping requesting that the American Lan Youjin be ordered to leave the country, in addition to the previous official letter to the governments of the four provinces of Suiyuan, Ningxia, Gansu, and Qinghai, recently sent a cable to the governments of the three provinces of Suiyuan, Ningxia, and Gansu, stating that according to a telegram from the Beiping Antiquities Preservation Committee and other five cultural institutions, the American Lan Youjin, without a government passport, secretly brought his wife and another American, Lu Gen, to Baotou in mid-May, carrying a large number of guns and ammunition, and planned to transfer to Wuyuan, Ningxia, Wufosi, Lanzhou, Liangzhou, Xining, and other places. They requested that the governments of Sui, Gan, and Qing provinces be quickly telegraphed to order him to leave the country within a time limit and confiscate the unlicensed guns and ammunition to protect the authority of the central government and avoid setting a bad diplomatic precedent. After checking, this Ministry previously approved a letter from the National Central Research Institute with the same content and forwarded it for review and handling. Now, based on the telegram with the previous information, a corresponding cable is being sent to inform you to investigate, order him to leave the country within a time limit, and confiscate the unlicensed guns and ammunition. Please reply.

Jiangyin Fifth Education Administrative Conference 165

Difficulties in Education Funding: Suspension of Enrollment at Rural Normal Schools. The Jiangyin Education Bureau held its fifth County Education Administrative Conference at 2:00 PM on the 27th, with Bureau Chief Wang Zhonglin presiding. Key resolutions: (1) The name of the Experimental Elementary School will be cancelled starting from the 21st year since it has not been approved by the Education Department. (2) Two central elementary schools will be piloted this year, one to be converted from the county-run experimental elementary school, and the other to be established by the Education Bureau in a suitable location in the countryside. (3) Xu Jiang, the principal of the Rural Normal School, proposed that 50 freshmen in the undergraduate program should be opened this year to complete the four-year standardization system. After discussion, due to the extreme difficulties in education funding in this county, there is no capacity for expansion. All enrollment at the school this year should be suspended. The rural normal school students come from poor families, and the food expenses should be changed to half the amount, with full food provided and verified by name. (4) Starting this year, schools with insufficient enrollment should be thoroughly reorganized by the Education Bureau. (5) The operating expenses for the Simple Science Museum will be provided from the arrears collected from various items such as the busy season grain tax. (5) The education budget for the 21st year was revised and approved. The meeting adjourned at 4:00 PM.

Local News

Labor University Faculty and Staff Protect the School Association Hosts Reporters Yesterday 166

Representatives Head to Beijing This Morning to Petition. The Labor University Faculty and Staff Protect the School Association hosted news reporters at the China Press yesterday. Chen Binhe from Shen Bao, Gu Zhizhong from Xinwen Bao, Zhu Qiran from Da Wan Bao, Shao Piaopiao from Xinsheng Bao, Fang Juying from Chen Bao, and dozens of Labor University faculty and staff, including Zhang Yuanruo, Tang Ying, and Han Yanmen, attended. Chairman Zhang Yuanruo gave a speech, saying that before explaining the work of protecting the school, he, on behalf of his colleagues, thanked the reporters. The association feels very fortunate that you have come. The association has been working on protecting the school for half a month. This protection of the school is neither to protect any individual nor to protect the status of the colleagues, narrowly speaking, it is to protect all the poor students of the school, and broadly speaking, it is to protect the entire Chinese labor education. This level should be observed clearly by people in society. The reasons for the Ministry of Education to shut down Labor University are nothing more than that the achievements are not significant, the equipment is incomplete, and the losses are too great. However, none of these are valid reasons. It takes a hundred years to nurture people, and the principle of education is like this. The Ministry of Education is too complimentary to say that Labor University, which has only five years of history, has made special achievements. In recent years, not only is there no achievement in Chinese education, but there is no achievement in everything. How can Labor University be solely blamed? As for saying that the equipment is incomplete and the losses are too great, and it is difficult to raise large funds to restore it, it is also an excuse. If responsibility is to be pursued, the first question should be why the Ministry of Education reduced and stingily issued the funds for Labor University. Labor education is the lifeline of China, where the rural areas are collapsing and the handicrafts industry is bankrupt, and it is urgently needed. The shutdown cannot be ordered on the grounds of financial difficulties and no funds for restoration.

Faculty and Staff Head to Beijing This Morning. The representatives of the Faculty and Staff Protect the School Association of the school, Zhang Yuanruo, Wang Wuyin, Tang Ying, Ma Shouzheng, and Zhen Jing, five people, took the express train to Beijing at 9:20 this morning (30th) to meet with President Wang of the Executive Yuan and Minister Zhu of the Education Department. At the same time, they also brought a petition from the association and letters from the 93-year-old Ma Xiangbo to President Wang, Minister Zhu, President Jiao of the Supervisory Yuan, and President Li of the Legislative Yuan for personal presentation, asking them to withdraw the order and achieve the goal.

Telegram from the School Protection Committee. The Express Mail Telegram from the Faculty and Staff Protect the School Committee of Shanghai National Labor University reads: All levels of party departments, education departments of all provinces, schools at all levels, academic organizations, newspapers, social organizations, labor and peasant associations, please note that labor education is the only opportunity for poor students to seek knowledge and the only organization to cultivate future citizens with both hands and brains. The collapse of rural China, the bankruptcy of the handicrafts industry, the decline of people's livelihood, and the weakening of the nation all rely on the promotion of labor education to revive. The colleagues of the school believe that educating for labor and laboring for production is the only way to revitalize the Chinese nation. Training for reproduction should be done in ten years. Schools should be industrialized, and students should be militarized to cultivate citizens who can win both economic and military wars. However, the Ministry of Education disregards the people's livelihood, ignores the nation, arbitrarily destroys labor education, and orders the closure of Labor University. It is the height of madness. We have always admired your righteousness and courage. Please resonate, quickly cable the Ministry of Education, withdraw the order, and extend great righteousness. Labor education is fortunate, and the poor students of China are fortunate.

Ancient Temple Bell Ringing Record (38) 172

— A Reclusive Husbandman Who Does Not Weed the Courtyard

On the morning of the forty-second day, I saw a piece of paper on Mr. Zhu's desk with these words written on it:

'"They don't want him in the city, so he ran to the countryside."

They say that, and it counts me as untalented.'

A person who has just arrived in the countryside and has received this blow, no matter how optimistic they are, it is always difficult to avoid some discouragement. Mr. Zhu, however, did not mind at all. At least, there was no hint of complaint on his face. The four lines of poetry he wrote seem as bland as rice soup at first glance, but upon careful observation between the lines, one sees a gentleman willing to suffer small losses active on the paper. I said to Mr. Zhu, "Someone once said, 'I will be a dragon or a tiger as people call me a horse or an ox.' The little poem you wrote has this kind of ambition." Mr. Zhu said, "I just wrote it casually as a reference for self-cultivation. It can't be considered any kind of ambition. But since you mentioned these two idioms, I would like to reverse them and use them as a motto for us to encourage each other. Dragons are mythical creatures, and tigers sometimes eat people. It is the oxen and horses that are the loyal servants of the people." After he said this, he picked up his pen and wrote:

'I will be an ox or a horse: Let people call me a tiger or a dragon.'

'What do you think?' 'Your revision allows me to see a new mission in the midst of glorious and bitter life. You have opened up an indescribable realm of wonders in the ordinary world before you. I have decided to follow you on a tour through this wonder.'

Although Mr. Zhu is optimistic, his work here has been met with great resistance. "The one in the ancient temple has no ability" has spread throughout the world, all the way to Zhang Huzi's tobacco shop. Bricklayer Lao Xu then allied with Zhang Zi to oppose Mr. Zhu, instigating parents and students not to cooperate with Mr. Zhu.

Australia's Hope 177

Sydney Dispatch. The Australian team selected to participate in the Olympics totals twelve people, eight men and four women.

Male Athletes. Only two men have a chance of scoring points. (1) Pan Ersai, who resides in Canada. Pan was the champion of the 1928 Amsterdam double sculls (one person rowing with two oars). Although Pan lives in Canada, he still retains Australian citizenship. In this year's competition, Pan can still win all long and short-distance boat races unless Pan has weakened in strength, in which case it should be considered an exception. (2) Swimming athlete Que Erden. In the previous competition, Que won second place in both the 400-meter and 1,500-meter freestyle. He went to the United States this time, not long after recovering from illness, but it did not affect his performance. In the Sydney Championship in January, Que's 800-yard result was 10 minutes and 22 seconds, only 1.3/5 seconds away from Kraebb's (US) world record. The hopes of the remaining six male athletes are very weak. Xu Huosi will participate in the 1,500-meter, but his mile result is 4 minutes and 20 seconds. The fact that Carlton, who is no longer practicing sports, is a major blow to Australia. His 100-yard result is 9.6 seconds, and his 220-yard result is 22.6 seconds.

Female Athletes. Of the four female athletes, two have a chance of scoring points. (1) Miss Wei En has hope in the 100-meter. Her 100-yard result on grass is 11.2 seconds, only 4/10 of a second away from Walsh's world record. (2) Miss Danis's 200-meter breaststroke is 3 minutes and 8.6 seconds, breaking the Olympic record by 3 seconds and Miss Xingdeng's American record by 1.4/5 seconds.

Wimbledon's Situation Changes Greatly, Japanese Sato Defeats Last Year's Champion Wood 179

Hills and Panlai Were Also Eliminated. London, 28th. The situation in the Wimbledon World Tennis Championships has suddenly changed due to today's results. The three most promising people to win the quarter-finals in the men's singles were all eliminated. It is even stranger that last year's champion Wood lost to Japan's Sato. The results of the four groups are as follows:

(1) Van Nies (US) Six to Two Maner (Spain) Six to Three Six to Two Seven to Five

(2) Crawford (Australia) Eight to Six Panlai (England) Two to Six Eight to Six Six to One

(3) Austin (England) Nine to Seven Hills (US) Five to Seven Six to One Seven to Five

(4) Sato (Japan) Seven to Five Wood (US) Two to Six Six to Four

Crawford Fought Fiercely to Defeat Panlai 180

Van Nies Defeated Maner. Van's powerful shots and cannonball serves were no match for Maner. Crawford and Panlai determined the outcome after a fierce battle. A portion of Panlai's previous... They were a championship athlete, but the Australian champion was not to be outdone. Crawford's performance was extremely excellent, with unparalleled accuracy. Several times, baseline corner kicks sent the line chalk flying. Many points were also scored by serves. When Panlai was tied at six to six in the last set and was leading by three points to one, there was hope of recovery, but unexpectedly, Panlai offered two consecutive sets.

Austin Returns to Original State 181

Austin's victory over Hills, who reached the finals last year, was greatly celebrated by the British. Austin has fully recovered to his original state and has a great chance of winning the championship. Austin constantly attacked with corner kicks, interspersed with extremely clever half-court balls and cross-court chops, leaving Hills with no time to respond.

Sato Defeats Last Year's Champion 182

Sato defeated last year's champion Wood. Sato's judgment was excellent, and his net play was perfect. In the first game, Wood did whatever he wanted, making Sato run around in exhaustion. As one set was about to end, Sato suddenly perked up, often intercepting the net and returning the ball without waiting for it to land. The competition in the second game was also extremely fierce, with both sides going up and down from time to time. Sato also won with seven to five. The third game was quite short. Initially, Sato was on the baseline, placing the ball left and right, very calmly. Wood ran east and west, unable to cope, and lost two consecutive games. But at this time, the momentum suddenly turned, and Sato sometimes showed slack. Wood won six consecutive sets and won the third game. In the fourth game, Sato won the first three to one, and five to four. In the last game, he won four straight to seal the victory.

Two, One Technique Record

Humility: Auspicious and Inauspicious 183

—

In the hexagrams and lines, there are both ill omens and auspicious signs, but only the Humility hexagram has all six lines being auspicious. People in big cities who use the characters for "humility" and "auspiciousness" in their names are numerous. To take just recent examples, there's Yoshizawa Kenkichi, who attended the League of Nations; Ueda Kenkichi, who invaded Shanghai; and Saito Kenkichi, who led the puppet state's athletes to Los Angeles to participate in the World Games. One Kenkichi here, another Kenkichi there, then yet another Kenkichi—it seems the three islands of Japan have become a production center for modest gentlemen.

However, examining their actions to see if they match their names, not one of them can be considered a modest gentleman. The first Kenkichi, at the League of Nations, turned black into white, acting inhumanely. Where was the humility there? The second Kenkichi led troops to Shanghai, engaging in a month-long battle. Where was the humility there? The third Kenkichi attended the World Games, preparing to expand propaganda for the puppet state and aid treason. Where was the humility there? The names of these three all contain the character for humility, but their actions are the opposite. Instead of calling them Kenkichi, it would be more honest to call them Fuken-kichi (Immodest Auspicious).

We Chinese, on the other hand, have many truly modest gentlemen. Those who declared long-term resistance have turned into long-term non-resistance. Why long-term non-resistance? Because they want to be modest gentlemen. Those who declared they would not submit to oppressive powers have now signed agreements. Why sign agreements? Only to be modest gentlemen. If that's the case, then the production center for modest gentlemen is not the three islands of Japan, but China!

However, the true essence of humility is that it should be directed inward, not outward. To act as a modest gentleman externally to the point of losing rights and national dignity is unacceptable! Such modest gentlemen are not within the scope of the Humility hexagram, and I fear all six lines would be inauspicious for them. Therefore, we have a definitive three-character assessment for China's modest gentlemen: Qian Bu Ji (Humility: Inauspicious).

On the Proportions of Tall and Short People 184

— Qingqu

Chang Shude from Henan Province recently came to Shanghai from Beijing to seek medical treatment in a hospital. Those who saw him were amazed, saying that he was not yet old but his height exceeded that of an average person several times over. He previously served as a flag officer under Ji Hongchang and as a clerk for the National Games in the capital. He reportedly ate one chicken and forty eggs every day, and also consumed twenty-four steamed buns for lunch. He could indeed be called a remarkable person. In contrast, there is the short person Tang Yisan, who is already forty years old but not even three feet tall. He is from Naxi County in Sichuan Province and resides on Avenue Joffre. He also once served as a military intelligence agent in Sichuan. For a time, the tall and short reflected each other, a rare occurrence. This was exaggerated into a curious tale and spread throughout Shanghai. I recall that four years ago, there was a tall person named Liu Ruqing who returned from the United States with a large fortune and lived leisurely in Beiping. Now, Chang Shude is also meeting people at the Rongji Great World to give a public farewell before setting off on a trip to various countries in Europe and America. Compared to the short Tang Yisan, he is no more than a sparrow under the eaves, chirping alone, looking up at the phoenix soaring into the sky. Anthropologists often say that people were tall in ancient times but are short now. There were those whose bodies covered several acres and whose one finger could cover Mount Taihang. The "Spring and Autumn Annals" mentions a tall Di named Qiaoru, but his exact height is not detailed. King Wen was ten feet tall, Tang was nine feet, and Cao Jiao was nine feet four inches. Yet, it is also said that "a child of five feet." The inconsistency of ancient and modern measurements is evident here. However, a person's height and the strength of their race are not without relation. I have examined that the shortest people today are the Eskimos in the northern regions of Australia and those who live near the northern part of Europe. They are just over four feet tall. People from Luzon and Malacca are also short. The black people in the southern part of Fiji who live in the forests are mostly only over three feet tall. The tallest are the Norwegians, the French Canadians, the red people of Canada, the Kafirs of East Fiji, and the Patagonians of South America. Australians are all over five feet tall. These are all compared using today's measurements. Generally speaking, this is the case.

However, there are those with exceptional natural gifts. In the thirteenth year of the Guangxu Emperor of the Qing Dynasty, a Greek man came to Shanghai who was over seven feet five inches tall. A French soldier stood shoulder to shoulder with him and was completely surpassed in height. An Austrian man was as tall as eight feet seven inches, and no one dared compare themselves to him. These are all recorded in the book "Thousands of Strange and Wonderful Things" of the Shanghai Machine Bureau, and can be verified. At that time, a man named Zhan from Anhui was also known in Shanghai for his height. Later, he was taken away by a Westerner and was able to travel overseas in luxury, returning laden with riches. At the beginning of his existence, who knows why Heaven bestowed such unique excellence upon him. It is said that a certain Russian man, already in his twenties, weighed only five French pounds and was just over one and a half feet tall. His father loved him like a pearl in his palm, often helping him stand on a table to play with him. His shortness can be imagined. The Japanese often call us "short slaves" and give him the epithet "many bumps." When the Japanese army invaded our city this time, apart from the old Dongyang (Japanese headquarters interpreter), almost all of them were robust and tall, superior to our soldiers. Experts say that their average height has increased year by year for the past forty years, and has now increased by as much as one and a half to one and six tenths of a foot. This saying is close to the truth. Alas, one can also gain insight into national character from this.

After Reading Chen Shuren's Art Exhibition 185

— Xu Shiqi

The art scene in the capital has been quiet for a long time. The vulgar world is like a hedgehog gathering, and our artistic spirit is bleak. As the intense heat spreads, our hearts feel even more parched. Fortunately, Mr. Shuren's art exhibition opened, so I accompanied Manhua to appreciate his fine works. The venue was the newly built National Assembly Hall of the Central University. The left-side upstairs and downstairs halls displayed dozens of works. Landscapes and birds-and-flowers each occupied half. The brushwork was gentle, and the style was unique. His paintings of Guilin's landscapes use a central brushstroke for outlining, with simple colors. The peaks and ridges are stacked, and the strange rocks are steep. I love his works "Solitary Beauty Peak," "Elephant Trunk Hill," "Fishing Boat on the Riverbank," and "Flying Waterfall at Dinghu," which use light and agile brushstrokes to depict the colors of the water and mountains, with a poetic flavor. My friend Mr. Binhong visited Guilin several years ago and showed me his works upon his return. I couldn't help but be fascinated. The Shanzi brothers, Daqian, explored Mount Huang, and Yu Zihua roamed Yandang Mountain with pride, looking up and down, capturing everything. Their works have long been seen by the Chinese people. Chinese landscapes, from Jing Hao and Guan Tong onwards, although giants have appeared in each generation, they have inherited from each other too much and lacked creative meaning. For an artist to strive towards the natural world is truly the only way to revive Chinese painting.

The most exquisite of the flower paintings are "Peach Blossoms Heavy with Rain," "Lingnan Spring Colors," "Pear Blossoms Heavy with Rain," and "New Willow" and "Spring Light." The colors are bright and moving. The space of a foot is filled with fresh air. "Lingnan Spring Colors" was exhibited at the Belgian Exposition, winning appreciation from Europeans. That year, I happened to accompany Mr. Minyi to Europe and participated in the event, having seen it before. I remember a poem inscribed on his "Spring Light" painting: "The heart for endless competition never ceases, Who is willing to come to the mountains and forests? It is pitiful that the spring light is infinitely beautiful, Only a small bird can appreciate it." The artist's calm mind can be glimpsed.

The Sanitation Undertaking of the Capital 186

— Huizi

Among the sanitation undertakings of the capital, the Central Hospital must be ranked as the colossus. The building materials for the wards were purchased from the United States. All operating expenses require one million yuan, which is organized by the Ministry of Health. Although the scale is large, the results are not good because the hospital has a very harsh rule: it does not accept serious cases. For example, tuberculosis is not incurable, yet it is also forbidden to be admitted. This causes much dissatisfaction among the people.

This year, cholera has spread very seriously in Nanjing. The number of people who die from typhoid fever each year accounts for almost sixty percent of the city's mortality rate. The Ministry of Health shirks its responsibility to the Municipal Health Bureau. Since the abolition of the Municipal Health Bureau, speakers all say that the Ministry of Health should be responsible. However, the spread of infectious diseases has become like a prairie fire. Alas, how lamentable! It is found that the allocated funds for epidemic prevention from the Famine Relief Fund and the Boxer Indemnity are no less than two million yuan for Nanjing alone. I wonder where this money is used.

The highest medical organ in the military is the Army Medical Department of the Ministry of Military Administration. It has achieved considerable success in handling the recuperation of wounded soldiers. There are many people who are jealous of the broad scope of the military medical field. They all want to seize a position in the Army Medical Department, but military medicine is a specialized field that cannot be accessed by ordinary doctors. Therefore, they cleverly establish titles and interfere under various pretexts. For example, the former Military Medical Supervision Department and the current Military Medical Design Supervision Committee are all motivated by jealousy. Thus, they spare no expense to waste national funds on these redundant measures. We can discuss matters impartially. Personnel can be moved, but the agency should not be changed. If the Director of the Army Medical Department is not handling things properly, then just replace him with a good director. Why set up a similar agency outside of an existing agency? Such as the Military Medical Supervision Committee in the seventeenth year, the Military Medical Supervision Department last year, and the Military Medical Design Supervision Committee this year. All of these are cleverly established titles, which only give rise to sighs of divergent political orders and criticisms of redundant structures. They are established and abolished suddenly, without any basis. This is simply treating national affairs like child's play. (No remuneration)

Short News 187

— Xun

Wu Letian of Pinghu, also known as Tianya Henren (Wanderer with Grievances), is a veteran in the sports world. In his spare time, he has a great love for calligraphy and painting, and is especially skilled in writing and drawing with a steel pen like a willow branch. Recently, saddened by the domestic warfare and widespread natural disasters, he is using his summer vacation time to create one hundred pages of calligraphy and painting fans. Each page is valued at two yuan, and all proceeds will be used for disaster relief. The general collection point is the gatehouse of Huizhong Middle School, Ximenwai Xieqiao, Shanghai.

A Record of Longing for the 19th Route Army 188

— Jingqing

The Shanghai United Association of Patriotic Organizations held a farewell banquet for the officers and soldiers of the 19th Route Army at the Great China Hotel the night before last. Toasts and cups were exchanged, and the hall was filled with people. The seating arrangement was in a mountain shape. The central chairman was Sun Bolan, an elder statesman of the Kuomintang. Although his hair was gray, his spirit was robust. On his left and right were Army Commander Cai and Brigade Commander Weng, among others. Their heroic appearance and spirit were admired by all. Their sincerity was unadorned, and their resolve was firm and refreshing, which was admirable. Their heroic discussions amazed the audience, proving that their reputation as famous generals was not unfounded.

During the banquet, Army Commander Cai gave a speech, saying that he would never forget the united assistance of the people of Shanghai. Even though the area was devastated, the people showed no resentment towards our army and people, and they mistakenly adopted false praise and over-praised us. His humility and deference were evident in his words. Brigade Commander Weng's words were mostly gentle. In conclusion, he said that the 19th Route Army retreated because it was exhausted of ammunition and lacked reinforcements, not because it did not resist. He hoped that the central government would consolidate the national defense of Fujian Province and pay attention to the air force. Staff Officer Qiu's words were very passionate and mournful, and he also cut sorrowful pears, which was quite appropriate.

That evening, a reporter asked Army Commander Cai whether it was true that the Communist Party in Fujian had heard that the 19th Route Army was coming and was willing to lay down their arms and cease fighting to show their respect. Army Commander Cai replied that it was hearsay and not worth paying attention to, which was also very touching. However, during the joyous banquet, there was still a sense of sadness and longing. Those who sincerely defended the country and were willing to sacrifice themselves were retained by the masses, who feared their departure. They only knew that the barbarians were fighting each other, exhausting the people to their advantage, and they were condemned by all. They only feared that they would not leave, and some even criticized them for being reckless and missing opportunities. This was also with ulterior motives and not worthy of emulation. From beginning to end, not a single arrow was added. The so-called long-term resistance, the entire plan was based on flawed assistance from Wang Shen, and the restraint was further met with setbacks. Even if Sima Yi exhausted his wisdom, it was difficult to resist Zhuge Liang's wooden oxen on the Wei River, eventually leading to defeat on all sides and failure. This is what is meant by Jingwei (a mythical bird) holding a grudge, unable to fill the sea of hatred.

These are difficult times, and worries fill our hearts. The scorching summer boils, and gatherings are not yet over. In the past, the famous gentlemen of the Eastern Jin Dynasty gathered at Xinting for a banquet. Looking around, they sighed and said, "The scenery is the same, but the mountains and rivers are different." They all looked at each other and shed tears. Only Wang Dao changed his expression and said sternly, "We should all work together to support the imperial family and restore our divine land. Why should we act like captives facing each other?" How is this banquet different from the banquet at Xinting? The invasion is deep, and the disaster is imminent. If we think of the loss of the Northeast, the ashes of Shanghai, and the lonely widows and bones of the fallen soldiers, the cyan pity and the blue blood, without having to present them to our eyes one by one, it should be like the strings of the door, weeping before playing. This is also lamenting the approach and unable to restrain oneself. Now the 19th Route Army is leaving, embarking on a long journey, their spirit like clouds, one journey reviving the summer, which is what we look forward to. From here on, moss marks and duckweed shadows, horse bellies and long whips, what year will the hostel and the hall, the turban and the seats share together? We look south, with endless longing.

Six Fen Eight Li Eight Hao and a Half

Vigorous Settlement of Securities Transactions In the morning market yesterday, because it was the settlement period for this month's securities trading, those who need to deliver goods must use spot silver to make up the difference. However, now, due to the current situation and the most intense price declines, short selling is not speculative. Therefore, there are only long sellers coming out, and silver continues to gather more and more. Even if the interest rate does not decline, it is difficult to stabilize, let alone when it is weak. Marseille Long Silk Waste Breaks 10 Francs 205

Silk Factory Long Silk Waste Only Offered at 9.5 Francs Per Kilogram: Marseille, France, is the central market for the distribution of silk cocoon byproducts from various countries. Top-grade silk waste from China and Japan is imported through Marseille and then transshipped to various ports. Recently, Japanese silk waste (i.e., silk head byproducts) has been sold off cheaply in Marseille, and prices have been offered upon request. As a result, our country's silk heads have been almost completely encroached upon, and market prices have plummeted. Silk factory long silk waste has broken below 10 francs per kilogram. White long silk waste (i.e., products from Jiangsu and Zhejiang) is only offered at 9.5 francs, while yellow long silk waste (i.e., products from Sichuan and Shandong) is only around 8 francs, a decrease of 45% compared to last summer.

Fifty Poems in Jueju Style (Continued) 208

— Meng Tiao Zhu

His bold pen and clear talent cannot be matched in the capital. Who can compare to him besides San Yuan? He should be compared to the three peaks of Mount Hua. His lofty standard cannot be shaved off from the heavens. (Zheng Taiyi and Zhang Guangya once compared him to the three peaks of Mount Hua.)

Bozi's poetry is poor, but he is known for his good singing. He looks down on all the ministers with white hair. His poems are full of tears for the people. He is not like an autumn insect complaining unfairly. (Fan Bozi)

The completion of the basket extension has not exhausted his strength. He also passed on the poetry criticism to compress the mountain. He has always been interested in the school of thought. He kicked over the altar of the Qianlong and Jiaqing emperors. (Chen Shiyi)

Yellow caps and court clothes chase after the ministers. The summer is light without a ruler. You were originally a beautiful woman, but you fought to be a thief. Can you forget your feelings under the Wu Mountain? (Fan Fanshan had a sentence after the national change: "The summer is light without a ruler.")

Donglang chants his beautiful words at will. He seeks the shadow of the past in his dreams. In the tall buildings, there are bright moons and singing. The poet is in despair every night. (Yi Kouchang Qinzhi claimed to be Zhang Mengjin in his previous life)

When he wrote to the point that his blue shirt was wet with tears. How many people know of the Jiangzhou school of poetry? He laughs at the unique Yunmen melody. It is still poetry after Mei Cun. (Mr. Wang Buyun, the father of Yuanzhong, is most famous for Caiyun Tune. Commentators say that Fanshan's two songs are still like Mei Cun, while Mr. Wang's is like Changqing.)

He mourns the water fairy in the autumn soul of the golden well. The mourning cicada's voice breaks in the Han Palace. When should he put down the pen of a talented person? Ten thousand red lotuses pay homage to the white lotus. (Zeng Chongbo's Gengzi Fallen Leaves poem was written for Concubine Zhen and was widely circulated. When he climbed the Guanyin Rock of Mount Heng, he saw the precious mountain, pearl palace, and blue sky inserted with the sentence "Ten thousand red lotuses pay homage to the white lotus." I especially love it.)

He initially escaped the name of the Party imprisonment. He returned to a hut for the rest of his life. He tries out his dragon-slaying skills. The first sound of thunder shocks the ground. (Huang Gongdu)

Science

Methods to Refresh a Straw Hat 209

— Ke

As soon as summer arrives, the sun hangs high in the sky like a fiery umbrella. We must use straw hats to protect our heads. However, white straw hats are easily stained with dirt, and straw hats that are one or two years old often turn yellow, and the color is not bright. Wearing them is not elegant. Now let me introduce the method of refreshing straw hats to the public!

(A) Washing straw hats: Preparations: (1) Sodium carbonate (i.e. soda). (2) Sal Ammoniac. (3) Sulfur (4) A wooden box with holes (5) Soft brushes (6) Gum water (This is not necessary) With the above items, first use a soft brush dipped in Sal Ammoniac solution to wash the straw hat clean, then immerse it in sodium carbonate (Sodium Carbonate Na2Co3) solution (about one cup of sodium carbonate, two liters of clear water), then rinse it with clear water. Before it is dry, quickly hang it in a wooden box with holes, and then fumigate it with sulfur. After two hours, take it out and rinse it again with a diluted soda solution, then wash it with clear water, and hang it in a ventilated place to dry in the shade. At this time, the hat is as white as new. If it is a hard straw hat, apply a thin layer of gum water after drying in the shade, and rub it hard with a cloth towel after drying in the sun, and the luster will be radiant, which is no different from when you bought it.

(B) Brushing straw hats: This method is relatively simple. You only need to dissolve calcium hydroxide (i.e. slaked lime Calcium hydroxide Ca (OH) 2) in warm water, and use a soft brush to brush it carefully with water. After brushing it white, rinse it with clean water, and hang it in a ventilated place to dry in the shade. However, everyone must remember to avoid exposure to the sun.

The above methods of washing and brushing straw hats are all based on chemical principles. The reason why straw hats need to be fumigated with sulfur before they are dry is because sulfur burns in the air, that is, the sulfur dioxide (SO2) gas can bleach, because the acid produced when it meets water can reduce the color matter. From this point of view, fumigating straw hats with sulfur is actually the most important procedure in washing straw hats.

Strange

"Talent" Stops Here! 210

— Song Lu

I remember in the autumn of last year, when Nanjing was busily preparing for the National Games, in order to make the venue solemn and majestic, a tall man named Chang Shude, who was eight feet two inches tall, was specially hired from Ji Hongchang's unit in Henan to guard the gate. At that time, I saw this news and wrote a humorous article called "Talent is Displayed" in a certain newspaper, and wrote the following crooked poem at the beginning:

"He is eight feet two inches tall, and he is frustrated; Once the opportunity comes, he will be a gatekeeper at the venue!"

The content was nothing more than talking to the tall man about many jokes and encouragement, pretending to use the present to prove the ancient; but the changes came, and there was no way to investigate. Since the September 18th Incident, the grand National Games has also dissipated into smoke! The "talent" of the tall man Chang Shude has still not been "displayed," so he is frustrated and almost unable to get a full meal, which is very pitiful!

Sure enough, "There is no need to worry about the usefulness of tall trees." The words of the ancients are true, and the huge advertisement of "Tall Man Chang Shude" suddenly appeared in front of my eyes! It turns out that the tall man has been recruited by the owner of the Great World, where he is "meeting the public."

In fact, this was also expected. Last year, I had already said that if the tall man has no way out, he might as well go to Mingxing Film Company to make a movie. Now the tall man does not appear on the screen, but shows his face in the Great World to be seen as a monster. Although the way out is different, the display of talent is the same.

Attracted by the power of the advertisement, I also spent two cents to admire this unique old tall man. When I stepped into the Great World and found the tall man on the third floor, the place of performance, I was disappointed again.

It turns out that the tall man cannot be seen for free. He is hidden in a small room, and another two cents for a ticket is required to appreciate his true face.

The tall man is also a "person." He also has eyes and a nose. It is said that besides being much taller than ordinary people, the rest is that he has a large appetite and can eat more rice than ordinary people. In addition, he has nothing else to offer.

However, the tall man is still a "living person!" So he can stir up people to go and see him. Otherwise, the Four Heavenly Kings of Lingyin Temple in Hangzhou are much taller than the tall man, so why doesn't anyone call them strange?

After seeing the tall man, friends who have not seen the tall man came to ask me, what is the tall man like? I said, "Talent stops here!"

Family Issues

The Old Man's Sorrow 211

— Tianfang

Old Zhang from the village, everyone said he was a lucky man. Four sons, three daughters, and so many grandchildren and nephews around his knees. A family of more than twenty people eating together, such liveliness, such envy!

Indeed, Old Zhang was very lucky. He lacked neither money, with over a hundred thousand in assets, he was considered the richest in the countryside; nor lacked longevity, at sixty-five years of age; nor lacked children and grandchildren. He fully met the ancient three wishes: "many blessings," "long life," and "many sons." In the eyes of outsiders, he should be very satisfied, what more could he ask for?

But in the desolate old man's heart, feelings of loneliness often arose, bringing boundless vexation. The eldest son was an official outside, said to earn over ten thousand a year, but the family had never seen a penny from him. In the past, when he was studying, he would ask for thousands of dollars at a time, but during winter and summer vacations he would always stay at home for a few months. Now, he doesn't even think of coming back for a whole year; even if he does come back, he leaves after three or five days, saying he is busy with official business and cannot stay long. It's as if he's a guest here. Times have truly changed. The second son is doing business far away in Zhangjiakou and cannot return often. Although the third son is at home, he spends the whole day outside, either playing cards or drinking with friends. When he does come home, he sneaks straight into his wife's room and never even asks how his old father is doing. Alas, they are all getting old! The youngest son is still studying in Beijing, like his older brother in the past, constantly writing letters asking for money. As for the daughters, there are three of them, and they are all married now. The eldest daughter followed her husband to Hubei to become some kind of bureau chief, only sending a few letters a year, or a little local produce, and has not been seen for a long time. The second daughter resented the meagerness of her dowry, compared to her younger sister, and was angry with her mother, refusing to return to her parents' home even for one night. The youngest daughter has a shop at home and has to manage family affairs and take care of her children, making it difficult for her to return. Alas, they have all flown away, leaving only eight or nine children who cannot fly away, still circling around you, wanting to be held and fed, and are very close to you. But, when your wings grow, you will also have to fly away from me! Although there are more than twenty people in the family, I am living a lonely life in solitude. Who says I am luckier than old man Li next door? He has two sons and a daughter, all living in the village, helping him farm. Although the family is poorer, they are all together, seeing each other morning and night. That is what is truly enviable! Alas, times have changed.

Excellent.

Kneeling and Crying Delegation 212

— Sun Guliang

Not long ago, various people's organizations in Tianjin, unable to deal with treacherous merchants who were trafficking in enemy goods, organized kneeling and crying delegations to set out separately and carry out kneeling and crying work. The goal was to warm the blood of the treacherous merchants, in the hope of achieving a unified effect of resisting the enemy. Although far away in Tianjin, closing our eyes and imagining it, the bitterness of their intentions and the desperation of their actions, this tragic feeling is enough for us to bear!

"Large quantities of Japanese goods are being imported," "Eastern goods are unusually active." In Shanghai newspapers, these records have recently often caught our eye. While enemy soldiers continue to massacre our compatriots, a portion of treacherous merchants have gone mad and are recklessly active! Under these circumstances, in order to alert the consciences of these treacherous merchants, it is very necessary to organize kneeling and crying delegations. We should all emulate the ten-day crying at the Qin court. We must cry to revive their hearts, cry to heat their blood. I think people are not made of wood or stone. When the nation is in imminent danger and their own deaths are at hand, they will certainly not remain indifferent!

First.

For the Lookout 213

— Hong

The Continental Daily News carried a piece of news the day before yesterday, roughly saying: "The Shanghai Municipal Council's fire department has set up the highest lookout post on the top floor of the Cathay Hotel, using telescopes to observe the entire city, which is very clear. Therefore, women bathing by the window in high-rise buildings should first lower the curtains."

The lookout post is for observing fires, not for observing women bathing. It's like comparing a horse's head to a cow's tail. Why involve women? Especially the sentence "should first lower the curtains" is the most incomprehensible. Whether women lower the curtains before bathing by the window has nothing to do with causing a fire. Public affairs are handled publicly, and private affairs are handled privately. Women bathing is a private matter, and observing fires is a public matter. The lookout watches the fires, and bathing is bathing. Not lowering the curtains is not to be seen by the lookout, but to ensure ample sunlight and prioritize hygiene. Is it possible that for the sake of a lookout, people should be prevented from maintaining their hygiene? I believe that the lookout is probably a romantic dandy, afraid that the lookout will see the beauty and forget to look out for fires, so this notice is issued, not for the sake of protecting women's dignity. Otherwise, why not say that men bathing by the window in high-rise buildings should also first lower the curtains?

This notice-style news seems not to have fully expressed its intention and should be changed to "Therefore, women bathing, changing clothes, and XX by the window in high-rise buildings should first lower the curtains." Because bathing should first lower the curtains, then why shouldn't changing clothes and XX?

Market News

Wuzhou Pharmacy Giveaway. The Wuzhou Pharmacy on Sima Road, recently, due to the irregular weather and the prevalence of epidemics, in order to promote hygiene and reward customers, has specially joined forces with the Tianhou Palace Bridge, North Sichuan Road, Xiaodongmen, and Penglai Market branches of Wuzhou in this city to hold a summer giveaway. All purchases of one yuan or more will receive practical gifts. Therefore, the retail departments of the pharmacy have recently been extremely crowded, and business is very brisk. The best-selling products are "Yalin Stink Water," "Liang Dan," "Mosquito Incense," and "Wuzhou Cologne."

Zhongxi Pharmacy's Low Prices. Since the Zhongxi Pharmacy on Sima Road started its low-price giveaway, retail and wholesale sales have been extremely crowded. The daily giveaway of "Mingxing Cologne" has reached over 10,000 bottles. Those from other cities who want to purchase "Mingxing Cologne" in large quantities must make advance reservations, as the number of wholesale customers is overwhelming. Although the pharmacy is rushing to produce it day and night, it is still in short supply. The sales of summer essential medicines, such as Baoming Shiyishui, have also surged, breaking the previous record for the highest sales in history. The pharmacy's low-price period ends at the end of this month.

Xi Jianyu, Zhang Abao, Xu Baotang, and Kong Abing, guilty of one count each of smoking opium substitutes, sentenced to one month imprisonment and a fine of ten yuan each. Wang A'san and Gu Pingfu, guilty of one count each of smoking opium substitutes, sentenced to two months imprisonment and a fine of twenty yuan each. Xi Jianyu, Zhang Abao, and Xu Baotang, all with two-year suspended sentences. ▲ Chen Shiying, guilty of one count of smoking opium, sentenced to two months imprisonment.
